\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}, {\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}, {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}. @nn

{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\bfseries{{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}}} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} {\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr}{\ucr} \doxylink{group___drawing_ga505f212582bf9b2bf95a4ef15f84af42}{tx\+Delete\+DC()}. ~\newline
 
\footnotesize When the program will be shutting down, TXLib will try to delete DCs which were not deleted, but this is not guaranteed.
\normalsize 
\end{DoxyWarning}
